# New Fish

Created from `newbiome.md`, now expanded across **15 biomes** in three batches.

Each biome contains exactly **300 fish** (20 rarity tiers x 15 fish), and every fish includes weight range and varied price range.

Total fish entries: **4500**

## Transmutation Tide

Fish count: **300** (20 tiers x 15 fish)
